          set cmd "set_attribute -objects \[$getCmd\] -name $maskConstraintName -value $value"

flags: ng [get_attribute $arg(-via) object_class]
  set objTypes [lsort -unique [regexp -all -inline {\S+} $objTypeString]]; # split string

  foreach objType $objTypes {
  # Validate that the object is a via
    if {$objType != "via"} { _error_user CMD-013 [format {"unsupported object type: %s"} $objType]; return }
  }

  set origCnt [get_selection -type via -count]
  set sourceVia $arg(-via)
  eval_with_undo -atomic gui_change_via_def {
    set via [set_via_def -vias $sourceVia -via_def $arg(-via_def)]
  }
  set newCnt [get_selection -type via -count]

  # If the object was selected and then was deleted, then re-select it here
  if {$newCnt < $origCnt} { change_selection -add $via }

  return $via
